# Visual Studio documentation for Microsoft C++

[https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/cpp-docs](https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs/cpp-docs).

Welcome! This repository contains source files for the work-in-progress Microsoft C++ 
(MSVC or Visual C++) technical documentation. The articles are published on the
[C++ in Visual Studio documentation site](https://learn.microsoft.com/cpp).

The documentation for Visual Basic and Visual C# are located in a separate repository at 
[https://github.com/dotnet/core-docs](https://github.com/dotnet/core-docs), 
and the Visual Studio documentation is located in the repository located at 
[https://github.com/Microsoft/visualstudio-docs](https://github.com/Microsoft/visualstudio-docs).
